# IH35 ERP — Master redesign checklist vs codebase

**Consolidated report:** For a single document with **changelog**, **recommendations**, and **verification**, see `**[ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_FINAL_REPORT.md](./ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_FINAL_REPORT.md)`**. Post-checklist / deferred work (e.g. open bills pager + selection model): `**[ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md](./ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md)`**. **Suggested QA when redesign is “complete” / before release:** `**[ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_POST_RELEASE_CHECKLIST.md](./ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_POST_RELEASE_CHECKLIST.md)`**.

This file maps the **consolidated master redesign** (Rules 0–24) to **this repository** (`public/*.html`, `public/css/*`, `server.js`, no `/src` React tree). It is the durable checklist the assistant referenced when uploaded lists lived only in chat.

**Implementation guardrails (not “authorization gates”):** Ship checklist work in **focused diffs** (UI, CSS, client JS, read-only `GET` additions). **Prefer** not mixing large **save/post/sync** semantic changes with cosmetic passes—when persistence must change, document it in the PR. **Do not** remove **application authentication**, roles, API tokens, or user-visible security controls. **Do not** remove form fields or **parts-map SVG** assets. **Architecture deferrals** (e.g. open bills pager + selection model) stay in `[ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md](./ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md)` until explicitly picked up. **Loads & dispatch board** (`dispatch.html` and **dispatch-only** styling): **lowest priority** — treat as **end-of-checklist** work; routine autonomous passes **skip dispatch-only** changes unless explicitly clearing a backlog item. **Hourly Word-openable progress report:** run `**npm run report:erp`** (writes `[docs/reports/ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_PROGRESS_latest.rtf](./reports/ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_PROGRESS_latest.rtf)`); schedule with **cron** per `[docs/reports/README.md](./reports/README.md)`.

**Architecture note:** The spec assumes `/src/styles/design-tokens.css` and `/src/components/StandardExpenseLines`. This app is **vanilla HTML + inline scripts + Express**. Equivalent locations are `public/css/` and markup inside `public/maintenance.html` (and siblings).

**Owner read:** Prefer the **scheduled RTF report** (`[docs/reports/ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_PROGRESS_latest.rtf](./reports/ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_PROGRESS_latest.rtf)` via `**npm run report:erp`**) for percentage + changelog + policy instead of chat-by-chat summaries. Routine passes still run `**npm run smoke`** when the environment allows.

---

Figures are for **planning and continuity**; they are judgment-based, not a contract metric. **200** card + **199** border + **198** typography + **197** **`maintenance.html`** remain; headline **~~66.3%** unchanged within rounding.

**Method:** Treat each rule **0–24** as **one equal unit** (4% of the bar each). Assign a **fraction complete** per rule from the status text below (Done ≈ 1.0, strong Partial ≈ 0.45–0.75, Blocked/Future without alternate path ≈ 0–0.2, Skipped-by-design ≈ 0.85–1.0). **Overall = average of those 25 fractions × 100%.**

**Intentionally out of this % (until product agrees):** items in `[ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md](./ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md)` (e.g. open bills pager + selection model).

---

## System inspection (high level)


| Area           | Finding                                                                                                                                                                                                      |
| -------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ |
| **APIs**       | QuickBooks and Samsara routes live in `server.js` (`/api/qbo/*`, maintenance/fleet/board APIs). Token refresh and error handling are embedded in those flows — **not re-audited line-by-line** in this pass. |
| **Forms**      | Primary ERP forms are in `public/maintenance.html` (maintenance, accounting, fuel tabs, uploads, etc.). Satellite pages: `banking.html`, `settings.html`, `fuel.html`, `dispatch.html`.                      |
| **Routes**     | Static HTML under `public/`; no client router.                                                                                                                                                               |
| **Smoke test** | `node scripts/system-smoke.mjs` requires a **running server** and network to `localhost`; it failed in CI sandbox with “fetch failed” (expected when server off).                                            |


---

## Rules — status

Legend: **Done** (meets intent in this repo), **Partial**, **Skipped** (already satisfied or out of scope), **Blocked** (would violate protection block or needs product decision), **Future** (large build).

### Rule 0 — Design system tokens

- **Partial (this pass):** Added `public/css/design-tokens.css` with spec-aligned **additional** `:root` variables (`--color-*`, `**--color-semantic-*`**, `--btn-*`, `--pill-*`, spacing, dimensions). Linked before `app-theme.css` on maintenance, dispatch, fuel, banking, settings. - **Spec path:** Use `public/css/design-tokens.css`, not `/src/styles/`.

### Rule 1 — Responsive layout

- **Partial:** `erp-master-spec-2026.css` + `app-theme.css` already enforce `min-width:0`, scroll columns, table wrappers for maintenance shell. ERP shell HTML pages use `**viewport-fit=cover`** so safe-area `**env()`** values apply on notched devices (**changelog 157**). `**banking.html`** inline `**.wrap`** no longer declares `**padding`** (including **≤900px**); `**body.banking-page .wrap`** in `**erp-master-redesign.css`** alone supplies `**env()`**-aware gutters like settings (changelog 177). `**dispatch.html`** `**?embed=1`** `**dispatch-embed-status-bar`** relies on `**erp-master-redesign.css`** for `**padding: 8px max(12px, env(safe-area-inset-right|left)) …**` instead of fixed `**8px 12px**` (**changelog 176**). `**erp-master-redesign.css`** `**body.dispatch-page .wrap`** third `**padding`** slot uses `**max(28px, env(safe-area-inset-bottom))`** so legacy TMS `**wrap**` rows that still match this selector clear the home indicator (**changelog 175**). `**erp-master-redesign.css`** maintenance `**.erp-main-body`** `**padding-bottom`** uses `**max(1.25rem, env(safe-area-inset-bottom))`** at default widths (**changelog 174**); **dispatch** `**#dispatchApp .erp-topbar.topbar`** horizontal `**padding`** uses `**env()`** (**changelog 174**). `**erp-master-redesign.css`** maintenance `**.erp-topbar.topbar`** `**padding-right`** uses `**env(safe-area-inset-right)`** at default widths (**changelog 173**). `**.erp-connection-strip`** + `**#authBanner.erp-auth-banner`** horizontal `**padding`** use `**env()`** in the global rules; redundant `**#authBanner**` `**padding**` in **≤900px** / **≤720px** blocks removed (**changelog 171**). `**erp-master-redesign.css`** `**#authBanner`** horizontal `**margin`** on the maintenance main surface uses `**env()`** with `**erp-master-spec**` padding (**changelog 172**). `**fuel.html`** **≤900px** rules no longer reset `**.topbar` / `.layout`** to bare pixels without `**env()``** (**changelog 168**).` **settings.html`** no longer applies fixed` *body`** `**padding`** on top of **`body.settings-page .wrap`** safe-area (**changelog 169**). **Reports** hub: at **≤900px**, toolbar padding and **`erp-reports-main`** vertical gap tighten slightly when the browse column stacks (**changelog 45**). At **≤900px**, maintenance **`.erp-main-body`** + **`.erp-topbar.topbar`** horizontal padding and gap trim slightly for tablets (**changelog 85**); those rules plus reports toolbar / roadmap / QBO strip / **401** banner now respect **`env(safe-area-inset-)`** on horizontal edges (**changelog 155**); **`erp-main-body`** **padding-bottom** respects **`env(safe-area-inset-bottom)`** at **≤900px** / **≤720px** (**changelog 157**). Module sidebar head / inner / footer padding trims slightly (**changelog 87**). **Dispatch** load-board **`.modal-bg`/`.modal`** and **`.wrap.dispatch-board-wrap`** use **`env()`** on host **`padding`** and **`max-height`** / wrap gutters including vertical insets (**changelogs 163**, **165**); **banking** / **settings** **`.wrap`** top and bottom **`padding`** use **`env(safe-area-inset-top|bottom)`** (**changelog 165**); **banking** / **settings** page chrome and **fuel** QBO strip margins tighten slightly on tablets (**changelog 88**); **company hub** QBO strip side padding tightens on tablets (**changelog 89**). **Fuel** fleet column chrome uses **`var(--color-border, var(--line))`** for shared dividers (**changelog 119**); **`fuel.html`** inline **`.topbar`** / **`.layout`** respect **`env(safe-area-inset-*)`** (**changelog 166**). **`index.html`** hub **`header`/`.grid`/`footer`** inline **`padding`** adds horizontal + bottom **`env()`** without duplicating top inset under **`board-nav`** (**changelog 167**). Dispatch/fuel/banking use simpler layouts.
- **Future:** Strict “no horizontal scrollbar at 1280/1440/1920” audit across every section tab.

### Rule 2 — App shell

- **Partial:** Maintenance uses `erp-master` shell (icon nav, sidebars, top bar patterns in HTML/CSS). `**erp-master-redesign.css`** **dispatch + fuel** `**.topbar`** bar `**color`** matches body / control ink (**changelog 192**). `**app-theme.css`** legacy **TMS** strip (`**body.dispatch-page` / `body.fuel-board`**, `**.topbar`**, `**.topbar h1**`, `**.topbar button**`, `**.tabs button**`) aligns `**--color-text-***` stacks with `**erp-master-redesign**` / dispatch satellite intent (changelog 192). `**erp-master-redesign.css**` `**body.erp-maintenance**` + dispatch `**#dispatchApp**` / embed shell typography chains `**--color-text-body` / `--color-text-primary` / `--color-text-label**` (and `**--color-nav-inactive**` on the icon rail) before `**--qb-***` so the ERP chrome matches satellite changelog 186 intent (changelog 187); dispatch `**#dispatchApp .erp-icon-nav__link**` now uses the same `**--color-nav-inactive**` stack as maintenance (changelog 188). `**board-nav.css**` owns the workspace strip `**font-family**` stack (changelog 184); `**erp-master-spec**` no longer repeats `**font-family**` on `**body.fuel-board` / `banking-page` / `settings-page` / `dispatch-page**` `**.board-nav-wrap**`. `**banking.html**` satellite `**.wrap**` padding lives only in `**erp-master-redesign.css**` (changelog 177). `**dispatch.html**` `**?embed=1**` removes duplicate embed topbar `**padding**` now owned by `**body.dispatch-page #dispatchApp .erp-topbar.topbar**` (changelog 176). `**erp-master-redesign.css**` embed `**#dispatchApp .dispatch-embed-status-bar**` matches that horizontal inset pattern (changelog 176). `**erp-master-redesign.css**` maintenance `**.erp-main-body**` `**padding-bottom**` uses `**max(1.25rem, env(safe-area-inset-bottom))**` at default widths (changelog 174); dispatch `**#dispatchApp .erp-topbar.topbar**` horizontal `**padding**` uses `**env()**` (changelog 174). `**erp-master-redesign.css**` `**#authBanner**` on `**.erp-main-surface**` uses horizontal `**margin**` `**max(1.25rem, env(safe-area-inset-*))**` (changelog 172); `**.erp-topbar.topbar**` default `**padding-right**` uses `**max(1.25rem, env(safe-area-inset-right))**` (changelog 173). `**board-nav.css**` workspace strip (`**.board-nav-wrap**`) sticky `**top**` and `**.board-nav-inner**` gutters use `**env(safe-area-inset-*)**` on all surfaces that load the strip; hub ≤900px `**board-nav-inner**` + QBO connection strip horizontal padding align (changelog 160). At ≤900px, the left `**erp-icon-nav**` column picks up `**env(safe-area-inset-*)**` padding so the rail clears notch / home indicator (changelog 156). `**erp-master-redesign.css**` `**:root**` `**--qb-***` maps into `**design-tokens**` (`--color-*`, `**--btn-primary-save-bg**`, etc.) when that sheet is linked (changelog 111); dispatch rows in the same file lose standalone grays/blues in favor of those tokens (changelog 112); `**app-theme.css**` still carries a slim dispatch (TMS) strip — `**.topbar` / `.banner` / `table.data**` now use `**design-tokens**` fallbacks too (changelog 113). Lists & catalogs is a first-class Lists (**▤**) target in icon nav (and `**/maintenance.html#catalog**` + `**#catalog-***` sub-tabs); dispatch nav includes the same deep link. **Settings** uses the shared `**board-nav.js**` workspace strip (`**board-nav.css**`) like banking, fuel, dispatch, maintenance, and **company hub**. `**board-nav.css**` `**.board-nav-dd**` border prefers `**--color-border**` (**changelog 120**). `**app-theme.css**` `**:focus-visible**` uses `**--color-border-focus**` when tokens are linked (**changelog 121**); **maintenance** `**.topbar**`, **sidebar expand FAB**, **default buttons**, and **plain form fields** use `**--color-border**` stacks (**changelog 122**). `**board-nav**` dropdown link row dividers use `**--color-border**` (**changelog 123**). `**index.html**` hub header adds `**erp-help-tip**` for workspace cards + strip + QBO status (**changelog 55**); footer mileage / routing note uses the same `**?**` pattern (**changelog 67**); **company hub** `**board-nav**` strip + dropdowns use `**--color-hub-***` (**changelogs 70–71**). `**erp-master-spec-2026.css**` aligns **fuel / banking / settings / dispatch** strip typography with `**--font-spec-sans**` + medium-weight triggers (**changelog 83**). `**system-smoke.mjs**` includes `**GET /index.html**` shell checks (**changelog 67**), `**GET /tracking.html**` redirect target (**changelog 85**), and asserts `**topbar-hint-wrap**` on `**/maintenance.html**` (**changelog 86**). `**dispatch.html**` load-board `**<style>**` `**.modal**` + default `**.btn**` use `**var(--color-bg-card, var(--panel))**` for surfaces (**changelog 139**); **modal / stops / embed bar** borders use `**var(--color-border, var(--line|line-strong))**` (**changelog 140**); `**app-theme**` **dispatch** main board chrome matches the same stacks (**changelog 141**). Labels and module order still differ from the spec’s canonical list in places (e.g. “Fuel Plan” naming).
- **Future:** Align copy, dimensions (68px / 216px / 48px), and tab set exactly to spec.

### Rule 3 — Collapsible sidebar

- **Done (pattern):** Maintenance uses `erpSbGroup` / `erpToggleSbGroup` with `localStorage` keys `ih35_sb_*`. Not every sidebar in the spec has been re-enumerated item-by-item in this audit.

### Rule 4 — “+ New” menu

- **Partial:** Maintenance has a **+ New** menu; within each column (**Expenses & bills**, **Maintenance**, **Other**) menu rows are ordered **alphabetically** by label within **Standard** groups (**changelog 64** adds **Standard** / **Maintenance & fuel** / **Drivers** separators + specialized expense/bill shortcuts). Flyout `**width` / `max-width**` and `**#erpApp .erp-new-menu**` inner `**padding**` respect `**env(safe-area-inset-*)**` (**changelog 164**). Width/columns/custom fleet rows may not match the full 680px / three-column / custom-type matrix in the spec.
- **Blocked:** Implementing **new** modal types that change save endpoints would violate “no new backend unless instructed”; **UI-only** presets that reuse existing save paths ship as **dedicated modal entry** + hash routes (**changelog 64**) without new POST APIs.

### Rules 5–9 — Modal shells (Expense, Bill, WO, etc.)

- **Partial:** QuickBooks-style modals exist (`erp-qb-dialog`, maintenance work order / accounting flows). `**#erpDedicatedFormModal**` (`**erp-master-spec-2026.css**`) provides a dimmed overlay + scroll host that **teleports** the existing **Maintenance expenses** document shell and **Fuel manual** shell for focused entry (**changelog 64**); the host `**padding**` and inner shell `**max-height**` account for `**env(safe-area-inset-*)**` (**changelog 161**). **WO full-screen** modal shell + `**.modal-bg**` / `**.modal**` use the same `**env()**` pattern (**changelog 162**). `**app-theme.css**` `**.erp-drawer**` (right-edge field-help / add flows) uses safe-area for `**top**`, `**height**`, and `**__body**` bottom padding (**changelog 161**). Full parity with spec (duplicate Rule **5** chrome, unsaved confirm on every edge) is **not verified rule-by-rule**.

### Rule 10 — StandardExpenseLines component

- **Blocked / Future:** There is **no** `/src/components/StandardExpenseLines`. Cost lines are implemented in **maintenance HTML/JS** (`maint-cost-line`, etc.). Extracting a shared component would be a large refactor; **not started** to avoid breaking saves.

### Rule 11 — Pay bills

- **Partial:** Pay bills / QBO flows exist in maintenance + `server.js` (`/api/qbo/open-bills`, `bill-payment`, etc.). **Pay bills** open-bills grid — static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#bpOpenBillsBody**` for `**bpRenderOpenBillsPage**` `**innerHTML**` + pager (**changelog 361**). **Expense history** — static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#expHistBody**` for `**renderExpenseHistory**` `**innerHTML**` + pager (**changelog 364**). **Driver bill pay** — `**#accounting-driver-bill-pay**`, panel retitle + **Driver payees only** chip, **client-side** filter on loaded open bills vs `**/api/maintenance/vendor-catalog**` driver `**qboVendorId**` set (**changelog 64**); open-bills **pager + selection** model still deferred per `[ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md](./ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_DEFERRED_AFTER_CHECKLIST.md)`.

**Expense history** log — static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#expHistBody**` (**changelog 364**); **Live QuickBooks Master** vendor/item/account card columns — static leads + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#qboVendorList**` / `**#qboItemList**` / `**#qboAccountList**` (**changelog 366**); accounting **dash card** subcopy uses `**var(--color-text-body)**` / link color `**var(--color-border-focus)**` where updated. `**#authBanner**` (401 “login required”) uses class `**erp-auth-banner**` with **token-backed** warning strip styling in `**erp-master-spec-2026.css**` on **maintenance** and **banking** (replaces banking’s prior inline red strip). **QuickBooks Live Master** uses title `**erp-help-tip**` and shorter vendor intro (**changelog 47**); confirm with UX pass.

### Rule 14 — Upload center

- **Partial:** Tabs and import flows exist; **Upload center** main panel title + `**erp-help-tip**` on one row (**changelog 61**); **?** + one-line intro on **every** upload subpanel (**Bank**, **Comdata**, **Fuel**, **AP**, **Maint history**, **Other**, **Connections**). Sub-tab buttons are ordered **A–Z** by label (**Bank CSV** … **Other**). **Connections** status cards + pills use `**var(--color-*|pill-*-*)**` (**changelog 81**). “Every tab fully functional” should be verified with manual tests and real files.

### Rule 15 — Samsara-style filter bar

- **Partial:** Filter patterns exist on several tables (see spec comments in `erp-master-spec-2026.css`). **Maintenance → Security alerts** uses `**mr-filter-bar**` + `**mr-filter-bar__grow**` / `**__right**` for search, window, severity, and **Refresh alerts**. **Lists & catalogs → Service types (DB)** adds `**mr-filter-bar**` + live name filter for the Postgres catalog admin table. **Reports → Maintenance detailed report** wraps unit/date/type/search controls in `**mr-filter-bar**` + `**mr-filter-bar__grow**`. **Accounting → Fuel expenses** ledger filters + **manual fuel / DEF** header grid, **Expense history** date/source/search row + preset buttons (`**mr-filter-bar**` + `**__grow**` / `**__right**`), **Reports → Settlement** trip **Load / invoice #** + **Run lookup** / **Download CSV** row, **Pay bills** vendor/payment composer + **Recent bill payments** log filters, `**fuel.html**` **Diesel purchase**, `**banking.html**` snapshot + suggestions rows, and `**settings.html**` **Employees** search + **Refresh** use the same `**mr-filter-bar**` shell (**changelogs 48–54**; `**body.fuel-board**`, `**body.banking-page**`, `**body.settings-page**` in `**erp-master-spec-2026.css**`). `**mr-filter-bar .btn` / `button**` `**:focus-visible**` uses `**var(--color-border-focus)**` on **maintenance** (**changelog 81**) and on `**fuel` / `banking` / `settings**` filter rows (**changelog 82**). Not every table has full chip + pager parity.

### Rule 16 — Safety / HOS

- **Partial:** Tables and pills exist in maintenance for safety/tracking; **Active / in service** tab **Active drivers** + **In service now** column titles include `**erp-help-tip**` (**changelog 61**); **HOS clocks** sub-tab adds a static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#safetyHosBody**` (**changelog 305**); sibling static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**.safety-active-grid**` for dual `**innerHTML**` hosts (**changelog 306**); **Tracking → Map** adds a static lead above `**#trackingList**` (**changelog 310**); **All tracked assets** / **Drivers** / **Yard & idle** grids add static leads above `**#trackingAssetsTableBody**` / `**#trackingDriversBody**` / `**#idleSnapshotBody**` (**changelogs 307–309**); **Shop** internal / external / roadside / parts queue tables add static leads before their `**tbody**` hosts (**changelog 311**); **Maintenance → Fleet table** adds a static lead above `**#maintenanceTableBody**` (**changelog 312**); **Safety → Fleet snapshot** adds a static lead above `**#safetyFleetSummary**` (**changelog 313**); **Maintenance → Shop / location** (`**#maintLocationBoardHost**`, **changelog 316**), **R&M** integrity (`**#maintSecurityAlertsBody**`, **changelog 315**), and **Units** picker (`**#maintenanceUnitList**`, **changelog 314**) add sibling leads; **Assignments** sub-tab adds a static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#safetyAssignBody**` (**changelog 304**); **Driver files** sub-tab adds a static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#driverFilesBody**` (**changelog 303**); column sets vs spec — verify.

### Rule 17 — Reports

- **Partial:** Reports hub shell in maintenance; **Reports** toolbar title includes `**erp-help-tip**` (sidebar vs hub tiles vs search — **changelog 62**); **Executive overview** panel title includes `**erp-help-tip**` (Refresh vs **Sync QuickBooks lists + activity**); **TMS**, **QBO**, **sync**, **IFTA**, **Maintenance spend by unit**, **Team activity & security**, **Maintenance detailed report** tab titles include `**erp-help-tip**` (IFTA / maint detailed body copy shortened + tip). `**loadTeamSecurityPanel**` renders **Configuration posture**, **ERP user activity**, **Security audit log**, and **CMMS benchmark** panels with title-row `**erp-help-tip**` (**changelog 60**). **Settlement** **Trip cost rollup** + **Loads with recorded costs (index)** panel titles include `**erp-help-tip**` (**changelog 60**); static lead above `**#settlementIndexBody**` + datalist rebuild note (**changelog 354**); static lead above `**#driverPaySettlementsBox**` (**changelog 357**). **Settlement** trip cost rollup uses `**mr-filter-bar**` for load # + lookup actions (**changelog 51**). **Settlement** trip TMS context box uses `**var(--color-border|bg-card)**`; **Driver pay settlements** panel title `**erp-help-tip**` + compact `**mini-note**` lines. **Executive overview** generated/cache line and **TMS** summary use muted token text; **TMS** not-configured / error and **Spend by unit** empty states use two-line headline + secondary (**Rule 22**). **Spend by unit** rollup table and **Maintenance detailed** cards use **Rule 23** pagers after **Refresh reports**; **Maintenance detailed** adds a static lead + `**erp-help-tip**` above `**#repMaintDetailBody**` for **`renderMaintDetailedReport`** `**innerHTML**` (**changelog 363**). “All reports on one page / remove links from other sidebars” — **not fully enforced** in this pass.

### Rule 18 — QBO GET endpoints

- **Skipped (different shape):** Catalog data is served via existing routes such as `**GET /api/qbo/catalog**`, `**GET /api/qbo/master**`, `**GET /api/qbo/status**` and cached in `erp.qboCache` — not the exact `/api/qbo/accounts` … list from the spec. Adding parallel read-only GETs would be **new API surface** (allowed only if product wants duplication); **not added** here to avoid confusion with existing clients.

### Rule 19 — Toasts

- **Done (this pass):** Global `**.erp-toast-host` / `.erp-toast***` styles in `erp-master-spec-2026.css`. `**window.showToast(message, type)**` and `**window.erpNotify(message, type?)**` in `erp-ui.js` (`success` | `error` | `warning` | `info`; `erpNotify` infers type when omitted and replaces legacy `**alert()**` across maintenance, fuel, banking, settings, dispatch). Host div on banking, settings, dispatch, fuel, maintenance, and company `**index.html**` (hub loads `**erp-ui.js**` deferred for future use). Fixed host `**top` / `right**` use `**max(14px, env(safe-area-inset-*))**` (`**erp-master-spec**`) and maintenance `**max(16px, …)**` (`**maint-accounting-ui**`) so stacks clear notch / Dynamic Island with `**viewport-fit=cover**` (**changelog 158**).

### Rule 20 — Button loading

- **Done (pattern):** **FIX 10** — `erpWithBusy`, `erp-btn--busy`, spinners in `erp-ui.js` + CSS. Applied on multiple async actions (maintenance save split, banking, settings, fuel, **dispatch** refresh / catalog / save / uploads / auto miles / QBO doc sync from modal, **row** Create invoice & Sync attachments, quick-add truck/trailer; status `<select>` uses `disabled` + `aria-busy` while patching).

### Rule 21 — QBO error banner

- **Partial:** QBO alert / sync messaging exists in maintenance (`**#qboSyncAlertBar**`). Banner is `**position: sticky**` at the top of the scrollable main column so users keep context while scrolling; `**top: max(0px, env(safe-area-inset-top))**` and horizontal `**padding**` use `**max(1.25rem, env(safe-area-inset-left|right))**` so the strip clears notch / island with `**viewport-fit=cover**` (`**app-theme.css**` `**.qbo-sync-alert-bar**`, `**erp-master-redesign.css**` `**#qboSyncAlertBar**`, **changelog 159**). Tier styling uses **design-token fallbacks** in `**app-theme.css**`; `**.qbo-sync-alert-bar**`, `**.qbo-sync-head**`, and `**.qbo-sync-meta**` `**color**` chains include `**--text` / `--muted**` fallbacks when `**design-tokens**` is absent (**changelogs 193–194**). Accounting nav badge behavior — compare to spec.

`**loadTeamSecurityPanel**` posture / roster / audit / CMMS panel titles + **?** (**changelog 60**); **Upload center** main title row + **?** (**changelog 61**); **WO** **Operational status** + **QuickBooks — posting header** + **?** (**changelog 61**); ### Rule 23 — Pagination

- **Partial:** `**erpPagerRender**` / `**erpPagerSliceRange**` for tables that were wired (**banking** suggestions, **settings** employees, **maintenance shop board** internal / external / roadside / parts queue tables with per-tab page state; **maintenance accounting → Fuel expense** grid with `**fuelExpensePager**`; **maintenance accounting → Expense history** with `**expHistPager**`; **maintenance accounting → Saved Maintenance Expense Transactions** card list (`**apTxnListPager**`); **accounting → Pay bills → Recent bill payments** log (`**bpLogPager**`, `**__bpBillPaymentLogAllRows**` + client filter); **reports → Settlement / P&L** load index + per-load line items (`**settlementIndexPager**`, `**settlementLinesPager**`); **reports → Maintenance spend by unit** rollup table (`**repMaintByUnitPager**`, `**#repMaintByUnitPagerHost**`); **reports → Maintenance detailed report** filtered record cards (`**repMaintDetailPager**`, `**#repMaintDetailPagerHost**`); **Lists & catalogs → Service types (DB)** (`**serviceCatalogAdminPager**`, `**#serviceCatalogAdminPagerHost**`, client-side name filter); **maintenance → Maintenance Table** (`**maintDashboardTablePager**`); **maintenance → Safety / HOS** tab: **HOS clocks** (`**safetyHosPager**`), **Active** / **In service** panels (`**safetyActivePager**`, `**safetyInServicePager**`), **Assignments** (`**safetyAssignPager**`); **tracking → Map → Units** cards (`**trackingListPager**`); **tracking → All tracked assets** + **Drivers (HOS)** tables (`**trackingAssetsTablePager**`, `**trackingDriversPager**`); **tracking → Idle snapshot** vehicles table (`**idleSnapshotPager**`, rows cached on `**idleSnapshotPager._rows**` for page changes without refetch). Not literally every table >10 rows.

### Rule 24 — Connection verification on load

- **Partial:** Global `**.erp-connection-strip**` inner horizontal `**padding**` respects `**env(safe-area-inset-*)**` on all hosts that use the shared class (**changelog 171**). Maintenance loads QBO status / sync alerts in the **sidebar** and embed bars, and hydrates the same **read-only QuickBooks one-liner** as satellites via `**#erpConnectionStrip**` + `**erpMountConnectionStrip('erpConnectionStrip')**` on boot (**changelog 65**). **Dispatch** loads the same strip above the board topbar (**changelog 66**); strip is **hidden** when `**?embed=1**` so the embed status bar is the only QBO line. **Company hub** neutral strip uses `**--color-hub-***` until QBO tier classes apply (**changelog 69**). `**erpMountConnectionStrip(hostId)**` in `**erp-ui.js**` + `**.erp-connection-strip***` in `**erp-master-spec-2026.css**` also run on **banking**, **settings**, **fuel**, and **company hub** (`index.html`) after load. `**.erp-connection-strip--ok` / `--warn**` tier borders use `**--color-success-border-soft` / `--color-warning-border-soft**` (**changelog 89**). **Dispatch** board strip default `**margin**` `**shorthand**` is ordered before **≤900px** overrides and includes `**env()**` so narrow viewports keep side insets (**changelog 170**). Default **fuel** + **hub** strip horizontal `**margin` / `padding**` use `**env()**` on wide viewports too (**changelog 169**). At **≤900px**, **dispatch** + **fuel** main-column strip `**margin-left` / `margin-right**` use `**max(12|8px, env(safe-area-inset-*))**` (**changelog 168**). Universal yellow **Samsara + QBO** banner on every surface — still **not** fully unified with maintenance’s richer sidebar text.

---

## Changes made in the pass that produced this document

1. `**public/css/design-tokens.css**` — Rule 0 token file (public path; spec’s `/src/styles/` noted as inapplicable); semantic status line colors (`**--color-semantic-***`); bulk `**maintenance.html**` inline `**var(--*)**` for errors, links, QBO banners, import failures (see changelog **29**).
2. **Linked `design-tokens.css**` in `maintenance.html`, `dispatch.html`, `fuel.html`, `banking.html`, `settings.html`.
3. `**public/css/erp-master-spec-2026.css**` — Global Rule 19 toast styles.
4. `**public/js/erp-ui.js**` — `window.showToast(message, type)`.
5. `**#erpToastHost**` on banking, settings, dispatch, fuel (maintenance already had it).
6. `**showErpToast**` in maintenance delegates to `**window.showToast**` when present (single toast implementation).
7. **Banking / settings / fuel** async flows call `**showToast**` on success and error (and banking uses **warning/info** where appropriate).
8. `**dispatch.html**` — Rule 22 compact intro + help tips; token-backed main column tweaks in `**erp-master-spec-2026.css**`; `**erpWithBusy**` on refresh, QBO catalog sync (toolbar), save load, doc upload, rate-con PDF extract, auto miles, docs-modal QBO sync, **board row** QBO buttons (invoice + attachments), and **quick-add** truck/trailer; status changes disable the row `<select>` while saving; `**showToast**` on those outcomes plus QBO invoice / attachment sync, `**patchStatus**`, and **openEditLoad** load failures; `**showMsg**` escapes text; manual refresh passes `**loadTab(true)**` so failures surface as toasts while the timer refresh stays quiet.
9. `**erp-ui.js` — `erpNotify(message, type?)`:** toast-first replacement for legacy `**alert()**` across `**maintenance.html**`, `**fuel.html**`, `**banking.html**`, `**settings.html**`, `**dispatch.html**` (with heuristic type when `type` omitted). `**index.html**` — shared `**design-tokens**`, `**erp-master-spec-2026**` (toasts), `**#erpToastHost**`, `**erp-ui.js**` for consistency if hub gains scripts later.
10. **Rule 24 + Rule 0 (continuation):** `**erpMountConnectionStrip**` + `**#erpConnectionStrip**` on **banking**, **settings**, **fuel**, **index**; token-backed `**--color-bg-page**` body background on banking/settings/fuel. **Rule 22:** maintenance **accident** WO inline help → `**erp-help-tip**`.
11. **Rule 22 (tire WO):** **Tire** record first-tire / same-invoice copy → compact line + `**erp-help-tip**` panel in `**maintenance.html**`.
12. **Documentation:** `**[ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_FINAL_REPORT.md](./ERP_MASTER_REDESIGN_FINAL_REPORT.md)**` — consolidated changelog, rule matrix, recommendations, verification, risks.
13. **Rule 23 + 22 (shop board):** `**maintenance.html**` — shop queue tables (**internal**, **external**, **roadside**, **parts**) use `**erpPagerRender**` with `**shopQueuePager**` state (default 15 rows/page; filters reset page). **Parts** tab intro uses compact copy + `**erp-help-tip**`.
14. **Rule 23 (fuel expense grid):** `**maintenance.html**` — `**#fuelExpPagerHost**` + `**fuelExpensePager**` slice the fuel expense table; `**postFuelExpenseToQbo**` reads ERP row + draft when the row is not on the current page so **Record filtered to QuickBooks** still posts the full filtered set.
15. **Rule 23 (expense history):** `**maintenance.html**` — `**#expHistPagerHost**` + `**expHistPager**` paginate the combined expense history table; **Export filtered CSV** still uses the full filtered row set.

## Product / engineering notes (optional; not blockers for checklist work)

1. **Priorities:** Which rules are mandatory for the next release vs nice-to-have (spec asks for everything at once; engineering may still sequence).
2. **Rule 10 / React path:** Shared component + build step vs one canonical HTML/JS cost-line implementation.
3. **Rule 4 — + New menu:** Which rows are deep-links vs new modals (avoid new save APIs unless explicitly scoped).
4. **Rule 18:** Thin `GET /api/qbo/accounts`-style aliases vs documenting existing catalog routes only.
5. **Regression:** Run server + manual click-through + `node scripts/system-smoke.mjs` when convenient before release.

---

## Rules that are **large** or **platform-shaped** (why “100%” is staged)

- **Scope:** Rules 5–12, 17, modals, and layout restructures touch **tens of thousands** of lines in `maintenance.html` alone.
- **Persistence:** Big-bang **save/post/sync** edits are **risky**—keep them scoped PRs, not mixed with UI-only sweeps.
- **No `/src` tree:** StandardExpenseLines as a separate framework component **does not apply** without a broader platform decision.
- **Verification:** Full QBO/Samsara click-through requires a **running environment** and credentials—not fully automated in CI.

---

## Reminder (uploaded lists)

If a newer checklist lives **outside** this repo, add it under `docs/` or paste unchecked items into a GitHub issue / this file’s appendix so implementation can be traced rule-by-rule.
